The Truth about the Lemon-Musk interview Anonymous ID:g1CwTlEX Sat 23 Mar 2024 06:36:14 No.462663585  Replies: 13 ViewReport
In Don Lemon's recent interview with Musk, Lemon put forward the argument that empirically, as pilots and air traffic controllers got more diverse, airline safety improved. This is a garbage argument, as I will explain.

The Civil Rights Act was passed in 1964. This banned discrimination, but did not mandate DEI (yet). This meant meritocracy. Genuinely talented Blacks and other people of color could rise up the corporate ladder.

However, after some time, the proportion of Black pilots and air traffic controllers stopped increasing. Even more disturbingly, the proportion of Blacks and POC in skilled jobs remained far below their proportion in society as a whole.

There are two explanations for this. One, systemic racism. Two, Blacks and POC are genetically, on average, dumber than Whites.

Based on data from 1964 to 2004, one can draw a positive statistical correlation between increased diversity and increased airline safety. However, Econ 101 tells us that correlation is not causation. The increased diversity from 1964 to 2004 was due to the meritocratic inclusion of genuinely talented Blacks and other people of color. On the other hand, the increased diversity from 2004 to 2024 was due to DEI mandates, as the proportion of Blacks and POC in skilled positions stopped increasing organically.

Here's the kicker: one cannot make a good argument against DEI without invoking the Hitlerian fact that Blacks are genetically, on average, dumber than Whites.
